## <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="7edf7-1787">Commenti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7edf7-1787">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7edf7-1788">La classe **MS-DFSR-Subscription** fa parte del supporto del servizio di replica file System distribuito (DFS).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7edf7-1788">The **ms-DFSR-Subscription** class is a part of the Distributed File System (DFS) Replication service support.</span></span>
